     <br>
     <hr> 
     <p>Class for retrieving various kinds of information related to the application packages that are currently installed on the device. You can find this class through <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/Context.html#getPackageManager()">getPackageManager()</a></code>. </p>

     <!-- ========= ENUM CONSTANTS DETAIL ======== --> 
     <h2 class="api-section">Constants</h2> 
     <a name="COMPONENT_ENABLED_STATE_DEFAULT"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-1"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">COMPONENT_ENABLED_STATE_DEFAULT</h3> 
      <div class="api-level">
        added in 
       <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 1</a> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
int COMPONENT_ENABLED_STATE_DEFAULT</pre> 
      <p>Flag for <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#setApplicationEnabledSetting(java.lang.String, int, int)">setApplicationEnabledSetting(String, int, int)</a></code> and <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#setComponentEnabledSetting(android.content.ComponentName, int, int)">setComponentEnabledSetting(ComponentName, int, int)</a></code>: This component or application is in its default enabled state (as specified in its manifest). </p>
      <p> Explicitly setting the component state to this value restores it's enabled state to whatever is set in the manifest. </p>
      <p></p> 
      <p>Constant Value: 0 (0x00000000) </p>
     </div> 
     <a name="COMPONENT_ENABLED_STATE_DISABLED"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-1"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">COMPONENT_ENABLED_STATE_DISABLED</h3> 
      <div class="api-level">
        added in 
       <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 1</a> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
int COMPONENT_ENABLED_STATE_DISABLED</pre> 
      <p>Flag for <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#setApplicationEnabledSetting(java.lang.String, int, int)">setApplicationEnabledSetting(String, int, int)</a></code> and <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#setComponentEnabledSetting(android.content.ComponentName, int, int)">setComponentEnabledSetting(ComponentName, int, int)</a></code>: This component or application has been explicitly disabled, regardless of what it has specified in its manifest. </p>
      <p></p> 
      <p>Constant Value: 2 (0x00000002) </p>
     </div> 
     <a name="COMPONENT_ENABLED_STATE_DISABLED_UNTIL_USED"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-18"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">COMPONENT_ENABLED_STATE_DISABLED_UNTIL_USED</h3> 
      <div class="api-level">
        added in 
       <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 18</a> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
int COMPONENT_ENABLED_STATE_DISABLED_UNTIL_USED</pre> 
      <p>Flag for <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#setApplicationEnabledSetting(java.lang.String, int, int)">setApplicationEnabledSetting(String, int, int)</a></code> only: This application should be considered, until the point where the user actually wants to use it. This means that it will not normally show up to the user (such as in the launcher), but various parts of the user interface can use <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#GET_DISABLED_UNTIL_USED_COMPONENTS">GET_DISABLED_UNTIL_USED_COMPONENTS</a></code> to still see it and allow the user to select it (as for example an IME, device admin, etc). Such code, once the user has selected the app, should at that point also make it enabled. This option currently <strong>can not</strong> be used with <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#setComponentEnabledSetting(android.content.ComponentName, int, int)">setComponentEnabledSetting(ComponentName, int, int)</a></code>. </p>
      <p></p> 
      <p>Constant Value: 4 (0x00000004) </p>

For instance, the device might use a mouse or remote control to drive a cursor, and emulate basic touch pointer events like down, up, drag, etc. All devices that support android.hardware.touchscreen or a sub-feature are presumed to also support faketouch. </p>

     <a name="FEATURE_FAKETOUCH_MULTITOUCH_DISTINCT"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-13"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">FEATURE_FAKETOUCH_MULTITOUCH_DISTINCT</h3> 
      <div class="api-level">
        added in 
       <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 13</a> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> FEATURE_FAKETOUCH_MULTITOUCH_DISTINCT</pre> 
      <p>Feature for <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#getSystemAvailableFeatures()">getSystemAvailableFeatures()</a></code> and <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#hasSystemFeature(java.lang.String)">hasSystemFeature(String)</a></code>: The device does not have a touch screen, but does support touch emulation for basic events that supports distinct tracking of two or more fingers. This is an extension of <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#FEATURE_FAKETOUCH">FEATURE_FAKETOUCH</a></code> for input devices with this capability. Note that unlike a distinct multitouch screen as defined by <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#FEATURE_TOUCHSCREEN_MULTITOUCH_DISTINCT">FEATURE_TOUCHSCREEN_MULTITOUCH_DISTINCT</a></code>, these kinds of input devices will not actually provide full two-finger gestures since the input is being transformed to cursor movement on the screen. That is, single finger gestures will move a cursor; two-finger swipes will result in single-finger touch events; other two-finger gestures will result in the corresponding two-finger touch event. </p>
      <p></p> 
      <p>Constant Value: "android.hardware.faketouch.multitouch.distinct" </p>
     </div> 
     <a name="FEATURE_FAKETOUCH_MULTITOUCH_JAZZHAND"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-13"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">FEATURE_FAKETOUCH_MULTITOUCH_JAZZHAND</h3> 
      <div class="api-level">

This is an extension of <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#FEATURE_FAKETOUCH">FEATURE_FAKETOUCH</a></code> for input devices with this capability. Note that unlike a multitouch screen as defined by <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#FEATURE_TOUCHSCREEN_MULTITOUCH_JAZZHAND">FEATURE_TOUCHSCREEN_MULTITOUCH_JAZZHAND</a></code>, not all two finger gestures can be detected due to the limitations described for <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#FEATURE_FAKETOUCH_MULTITOUCH_DISTINCT">FEATURE_FAKETOUCH_MULTITOUCH_DISTINCT</a></code>. </p>

      <div class="api-level">

      </div>

      <p>Feature for <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#getSystemAvailableFeatures()">getSystemAvailableFeatures()</a></code> and <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#hasSystemFeature(java.lang.String)">hasSystemFeature(String)</a></code>: The device implements an optimized mode for virtual reality (VR) applications that handles stereoscopic rendering of notifications, and disables most monocular system UI components while a VR application has user focus. Devices declaring this feature must include an application implementing a <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/service/vr/VrListenerService.html">VrListenerService</a></code> that can be targeted by VR applications via <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/app/Activity.html#setVrModeEnabled(boolean, android.content.ComponentName)">setVrModeEnabled(boolean, ComponentName)</a></code>. </p>
      <p></p>

     <a name="FEATURE_VR_MODE_HIGH_PERFORMANCE"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-24"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">FEATURE_VR_MODE_HIGH_PERFORMANCE</h3> 
      <div class="api-level">
        added in 
       <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 24</a> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> FEATURE_VR_MODE_HIGH_PERFORMANCE</pre> 
      <p>Feature for <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#getSystemAvailableFeatures()">getSystemAvailableFeatures()</a></code> and <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#hasSystemFeature(java.lang.String)">hasSystemFeature(String)</a></code>: The device implements <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#FEATURE_VR_MODE">FEATURE_VR_MODE</a></code> but additionally meets extra CDD requirements to provide a high-quality VR experience. In general, devices declaring this feature will additionally: </p>
      <ul> 
       <li>Deliver consistent performance at a high framerate over an extended period of time for typical VR application CPU/GPU workloads with a minimal number of frame drops for VR applications that have called <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/view/Window.html#setSustainedPerformanceMode(boolean)">setSustainedPerformanceMode(boolean)</a></code>.</li> 
       <li>Implement <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#FEATURE_HIFI_SENSORS">FEATURE_HIFI_SENSORS</a></code> and have a low sensor latency.</li> 
       <li>Include optimizations to lower display persistence while running VR applications.</li> 
       <li>Implement an optimized render path to minimize latency to draw to the device's main display.</li> 
       <li>Include the following EGL extensions: EGL_ANDROID_create_native_client_buffer, EGL_ANDROID_front_buffer_auto_refresh, EGL_EXT_protected_content, EGL_KHR_mutable_render_buffer, EGL_KHR_reusable_sync, and EGL_KHR_wait_sync.</li> 
       <li>Provide at least one CPU core that is reserved for use solely by the top, foreground VR application process for critical render threads while such an application is running.</li> 
      </ul> 
      <p></p>
      <p></p> 
      <p>Constant Value: "android.hardware.vr.high_performance" </p>
     </div> 
     <a name="FEATURE_VULKAN_HARDWARE_COMPUTE"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-26"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">FEATURE_VULKAN_HARDWARE_COMPUTE</h3> 
      <div class="api-level">
        added in 
       <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 26</a> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> FEATURE_VULKAN_HARDWARE_COMPUTE</pre> 
      <p>Feature for <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#getSystemAvailableFeatures()">getSystemAvailableFeatures()</a></code> and <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#hasSystemFeature(java.lang.String, int)">hasSystemFeature(String, int)</a></code>: If this feature is supported, the Vulkan native API will enumerate at least one <code>VkPhysicalDevice</code>, and the feature version will indicate what level of optional compute features are supported beyond the Vulkan 1.0 requirements. </p>
      <p> Compute level 0 indicates support for the <code>VariablePointers</code> SPIR-V capability defined by the SPV_KHR_variable_pointers extension. </p>
      <p></p> 
      <p>Constant Value: "android.hardware.vulkan.compute" </p>
     </div> 
     <a name="FEATURE_VULKAN_HARDWARE_LEVEL"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-24"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">FEATURE_VULKAN_HARDWARE_LEVEL</h3> 
      <div class="api-level">
        added in 
       <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 24</a> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> FEATURE_VULKAN_HARDWARE_LEVEL</pre> 
      <p>Feature for <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#getSystemAvailableFeatures()">getSystemAvailableFeatures()</a></code> and <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#hasSystemFeature(java.lang.String, int)">hasSystemFeature(String, int)</a></code>: If this feature is supported, the Vulkan native API will enumerate at least one <code>VkPhysicalDevice</code>, and the feature version will indicate what level of optional hardware features limits it supports. </p>
      <p> Level 0 includes the base Vulkan requirements as well as: </p>
      <ul>
       <li><code>VkPhysicalDeviceFeatures::textureCompressionETC2</code></li>
      </ul> 
      <p> Level 1 additionally includes: </p>
      <ul> 
       <li><code>VkPhysicalDeviceFeatures::fullDrawIndexUint32</code></li> 
       <li><code>VkPhysicalDeviceFeatures::imageCubeArray</code></li> 
       <li><code>VkPhysicalDeviceFeatures::independentBlend</code></li> 
       <li><code>VkPhysicalDeviceFeatures::geometryShader</code></li> 
       <li><code>VkPhysicalDeviceFeatures::tessellationShader</code></li> 
       <li><code>VkPhysicalDeviceFeatures::sampleRateShading</code></li> 
       <li><code>VkPhysicalDeviceFeatures::textureCompressionASTC_LDR</code></li> 
       <li><code>VkPhysicalDeviceFeatures::fragmentStoresAndAtomics</code></li> 
       <li><code>VkPhysicalDeviceFeatures::shaderImageGatherExtended</code></li> 
       <li><code>VkPhysicalDeviceFeatures::shaderUniformBufferArrayDynamicIndexing</code></li> 
       <li><code>VkPhysicalDeviceFeatures::shaderSampledImageArrayDynamicIndexing</code></li> 
      </ul> 
      <p></p>
      <p></p> 
      <p>Constant Value: "android.hardware.vulkan.level" </p>
     </div> 
     <a name="FEATURE_VULKAN_HARDWARE_VERSION"></a>

      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> FEATURE_VULKAN_HARDWARE_VERSION</pre> 
      <p>Feature for <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#getSystemAvailableFeatures()">getSystemAvailableFeatures()</a></code> and <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#hasSystemFeature(java.lang.String, int)">hasSystemFeature(String, int)</a></code>: The version of this feature indicates the highest <code>VkPhysicalDeviceProperties::apiVersion</code> supported by the physical devices that support the hardware level indicated by <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#FEATURE_VULKAN_HARDWARE_LEVEL">FEATURE_VULKAN_HARDWARE_LEVEL</a></code>. The feature version uses the same encoding as Vulkan version numbers: </p>
      <ul> 
       <li>Major version number in bits 31-22</li> 
       <li>Minor version number in bits 21-12</li> 
       <li>Patch version number in bits 11-0</li> 
      </ul> 
      <p></p>
      <p></p> 
      <p>Constant Value: "android.hardware.vulkan.version" </p>
     </div>

      <p>Resolution and querying flag: if set, only filters that support the <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/Intent.html#CATEGORY_DEFAULT">CATEGORY_DEFAULT</a></code> will be considered for matching. This is a synonym for including the CATEGORY_DEFAULT in your supplied Intent. </p>
      <p></p> 
      <p>Constant Value: 65536 (0x00010000) </p>
     </div> 
     <a name="MATCH_DIRECT_BOOT_AWARE"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-24"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">MATCH_DIRECT_BOOT_AWARE</h3> 
      <div class="api-level">
        added in 
       <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 24</a> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
int MATCH_DIRECT_BOOT_AWARE</pre> 
      <p>Querying flag: match components which are direct boot <em>aware</em> in the returned info, regardless of the current user state. </p>
      <p> When neither <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DIRECT_BOOT_AWARE">MATCH_DIRECT_BOOT_AWARE</a></code> nor <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DIRECT_BOOT_UNAWARE">MATCH_DIRECT_BOOT_UNAWARE</a></code> are specified, the default behavior is to match only runnable components based on the user state. For example, when a user is started but credentials have not been presented yet, the user is running "locked" and only <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DIRECT_BOOT_AWARE">MATCH_DIRECT_BOOT_AWARE</a></code> components are returned. Once the user credentials have been presented, the user is running "unlocked" and both <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DIRECT_BOOT_AWARE">MATCH_DIRECT_BOOT_AWARE</a></code> and <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DIRECT_BOOT_UNAWARE">MATCH_DIRECT_BOOT_UNAWARE</a></code> components are returned.</p>
      <p></p> 
      <div> 
       <p><b>See also:</b></p> 
       <ul class="nolist">
        <li><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/os/UserManager.html#isUserUnlocked()">isUserUnlocked()</a></code></li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
      <p>Constant Value: 524288 (0x00080000) </p>
     </div>

      <p> </p>

     <a name="addPermission(android.content.pm.PermissionInfo)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-1"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">addPermission</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 1</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
boolean addPermission (<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PermissionInfo.html">PermissionInfo</a> info)</pre> 
      <p>Add a new dynamic permission to the system. For this to work, your package must have defined a permission tree through the <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/R.styleable.html#AndroidManifestPermissionTree">&lt;permission-tree&gt;</a></code> tag in its manifest. A package can only add permissions to trees that were defined by either its own package or another with the same user id; a permission is in a tree if it matches the name of the permission tree + ".": for example, "com.foo.bar" is a member of the permission tree "com.foo". </p>
      <p>It is good to make your permission tree name descriptive, because you are taking possession of that entire set of permission names. Thus, it must be under a domain you control, with a suffix that will not match any normal permissions that may be declared in any applications that are part of that domain. </p>
      <p>New permissions must be added before any .apks are installed that use those permissions. Permissions you add through this method are remembered across reboots of the device. If the given permission already exists, the info you supply here will be used to update it.</p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Parameters</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>info</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>PermissionInfo</code>: Description of the permission to be added.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>boolean</code></td> 
         <td width="100%">Returns true if a new permission was created, false if an existing one was updated.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Throws</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/SecurityException.html">SecurityException</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">if you are not allowed to add the given permission name.</td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <div> 
       <p><b>See also:</b></p> 
       <ul class="nolist">
        <li><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#removePermission(java.lang.String)">removePermission(String)</a></code></li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <a name="addPermissionAsync(android.content.pm.PermissionInfo)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-8"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">addPermissionAsync</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 8</a>

      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
boolean addPermissionAsync (<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PermissionInfo.html">PermissionInfo</a> info)</pre> 
      <p>Like <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#addPermission(android.content.pm.PermissionInfo)">addPermission(PermissionInfo)</a></code> but asynchronously persists the package manager state after returning from the call, allowing it to return quicker and batch a series of adds at the expense of no guarantee the added permission will be retained if the device is rebooted before it is written. </p>

     <a name="addPreferredActivity(android.content.IntentFilter, int, android.content.ComponentName[], android.content.ComponentName)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-1"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">addPreferredActivity</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 1</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
void addPreferredActivity (<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/IntentFilter.html">IntentFilter</a> filter, 
                int match, 
                <a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/ComponentName.html">ComponentName[]</a> set, 
                <a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/ComponentName.html">ComponentName</a> activity)</pre> 
      <p> </p>
      <p class="caution"><strong> This method was deprecated in API level 8.</strong><br> This is a protected API that should not have been available to third party applications. It is the platform's responsibility for assigning preferred activities and this cannot be directly modified. Add a new preferred activity mapping to the system. This will be used to automatically select the given activity component when <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/Context.html#startActivity(android.content.Intent)">Context.startActivity()</a></code> finds multiple matching activities and also matches the given filter. </p> 
      <p></p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Parameters</th>

         <td><code>filter</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>IntentFilter</code>: The set of intents under which this activity will be made preferred.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>match</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>int</code>: The IntentFilter match category that this preference applies to.<p></p></td>

     <a name="canRequestPackageInstalls()"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-26"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">canRequestPackageInstalls</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 26</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
boolean canRequestPackageInstalls ()</pre> 
      <p>Checks whether the calling package is allowed to request package installs through package installer. Apps are encouraged to call this API before launching the package installer via intent <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/Intent.html#ACTION_INSTALL_PACKAGE">ACTION_INSTALL_PACKAGE</a></code>. Starting from Android O, the user can explicitly choose what external sources they trust to install apps on the device. If this API returns false, the install request will be blocked by the package installer and a dialog will be shown to the user with an option to launch settings to change their preference. An application must target Android O or higher and declare permission <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/Manifest.permission.html#REQUEST_INSTALL_PACKAGES">REQUEST_INSTALL_PACKAGES</a></code> in order to use this API.</p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>boolean</code></td> 
         <td width="100%">true if the calling package is trusted by the user to request install packages on the device, false otherwise.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <div> 
       <p><b>See also:</b></p> 
       <ul class="nolist">
        <li><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/Intent.html#ACTION_INSTALL_PACKAGE">ACTION_INSTALL_PACKAGE</a></code></li>
        <li><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/provider/Settings.html#ACTION_MANAGE_UNKNOWN_APP_SOURCES">ACTION_MANAGE_UNKNOWN_APP_SOURCES</a></code></li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
     </div>

     <a name="checkSignatures(java.lang.String, java.lang.String)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-1"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">checkSignatures</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 1</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
int checkSignatures (<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> pkg1, 
                <a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> pkg2)</pre> 
      <p>Compare the signatures of two packages to determine if the same signature appears in both of them. If they do contain the same signature, then they are allowed special privileges when working with each other: they can share the same user-id, run instrumentation against each other, etc.</p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Parameters</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>pkg1</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>String</code>: First package name whose signature will be compared.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>pkg2</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>String</code>: Second package name whose signature will be compared.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>int</code></td> 
         <td width="100%">Returns an integer indicating whether all signatures on the two packages match. The value is &gt;= 0 (<code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#SIGNATURE_MATCH">SIGNATURE_MATCH</a></code>) if all signatures match or &lt; 0 if there is not a match (<code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#SIGNATURE_NO_MATCH">SIGNATURE_NO_MATCH</a></code> or <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#SIGNATURE_UNKNOWN_PACKAGE">SIGNATURE_UNKNOWN_PACKAGE</a></code>).<p>Value is <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#SIGNATURE_MATCH">SIGNATURE_MATCH</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#SIGNATURE_NEITHER_SIGNED">SIGNATURE_NEITHER_SIGNED</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#SIGNATURE_FIRST_NOT_SIGNED">SIGNATURE_FIRST_NOT_SIGNED</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#SIGNATURE_SECOND_NOT_SIGNED">SIGNATURE_SECOND_NOT_SIGNED</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#SIGNATURE_NO_MATCH">SIGNATURE_NO_MATCH</a></code> or <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#SIGNATURE_UNKNOWN_PACKAGE">SIGNATURE_UNKNOWN_PACKAGE</a></code>.</p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <div> 
       <p><b>See also:</b></p> 
       <ul class="nolist">
        <li><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#checkSignatures(int, int)">checkSignatures(int, int)</a></code></li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <a name="checkSignatures(int, int)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-5"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">checkSignatures</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 5</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
int checkSignatures (int uid1, 
                int uid2)</pre> 
      <p>Like <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#checkSignatures(java.lang.String, java.lang.String)">checkSignatures(String, String)</a></code>, but takes UIDs of the two packages to be checked. This can be useful, for example, when doing the check in an IPC, where the UID is the only identity available. It is functionally identical to determining the package associated with the UIDs and checking their signatures.</p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Parameters</th>
        </tr>

        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>uid2</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>int</code>: Second UID whose signature will be compared.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>int</code></td> 
         <td width="100%">Returns an integer indicating whether all signatures on the two packages match. The value is &gt;= 0 (<code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#SIGNATURE_MATCH">SIGNATURE_MATCH</a></code>) if all signatures match or &lt; 0 if there is not a match (<code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#SIGNATURE_NO_MATCH">SIGNATURE_NO_MATCH</a></code> or <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#SIGNATURE_UNKNOWN_PACKAGE">SIGNATURE_UNKNOWN_PACKAGE</a></code>).<p>Value is <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#SIGNATURE_MATCH">SIGNATURE_MATCH</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#SIGNATURE_NEITHER_SIGNED">SIGNATURE_NEITHER_SIGNED</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#SIGNATURE_FIRST_NOT_SIGNED">SIGNATURE_FIRST_NOT_SIGNED</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#SIGNATURE_SECOND_NOT_SIGNED">SIGNATURE_SECOND_NOT_SIGNED</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#SIGNATURE_NO_MATCH">SIGNATURE_NO_MATCH</a></code> or <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#SIGNATURE_UNKNOWN_PACKAGE">SIGNATURE_UNKNOWN_PACKAGE</a></code>.</p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table>

     <a name="extendVerificationTimeout(int, int, long)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-17"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">extendVerificationTimeout</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 17</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
void extendVerificationTimeout (int id, 
                int verificationCodeAtTimeout, 
                long millisecondsToDelay)</pre> 
      <p>Allows a package listening to the <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/Intent.html#ACTION_PACKAGE_NEEDS_VERIFICATION">package verification broadcast</a></code> to extend the default timeout for a response and declare what action to perform after the timeout occurs. The response must include the <code>verificationCodeAtTimeout</code> which is one of <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#VERIFICATION_ALLOW">VERIFICATION_ALLOW</a></code> or <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#VERIFICATION_REJECT">VERIFICATION_REJECT</a></code>. This method may only be called once per package id. Additional calls will have no effect.</p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Parameters</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>id</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>int</code>: pending package identifier as passed via the <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#EXTRA_VERIFICATION_ID">EXTRA_VERIFICATION_ID</a></code> Intent extra.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>verificationCodeAtTimeout</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>int</code>: either <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#VERIFICATION_ALLOW">VERIFICATION_ALLOW</a></code> or <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#VERIFICATION_REJECT">VERIFICATION_REJECT</a></code>. If <code>verificationCodeAtTimeout</code> is neither <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#VERIFICATION_ALLOW">VERIFICATION_ALLOW</a></code> or <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#VERIFICATION_REJECT">VERIFICATION_REJECT</a></code>, then <code>verificationCodeAtTimeout</code> will default to <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#VERIFICATION_REJECT">VERIFICATION_REJECT</a></code>.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>millisecondsToDelay</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>long</code>: the amount of time requested for the timeout. Must be positive and less than <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MAXIMUM_VERIFICATION_TIMEOUT">MAXIMUM_VERIFICATION_TIMEOUT</a></code>. If <code>millisecondsToDelay</code> is out of bounds, <code>millisecondsToDelay</code> will be set to the closest in bounds value; namely, 0 or <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MAXIMUM_VERIFICATION_TIMEOUT">MAXIMUM_VERIFICATION_TIMEOUT</a></code>.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Throws</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/SecurityException.html">SecurityException</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">if the caller does not have the PACKAGE_VERIFICATION_AGENT permission. </td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
     </div> 
     <a name="getActivityBanner(android.content.Intent)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-20"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">getActivityBanner</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 20</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/graphics/drawable/Drawable.html">Drawable</a> getActivityBanner (<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/Intent.html">Intent</a> intent)</pre> 
      <p>Retrieve the banner associated with an Intent. If intent.getClassName() is set, this simply returns the result of getActivityBanner(intent.getClassName()). Otherwise it resolves the intent's component and returns the banner associated with the resolved component. If intent.getClassName() cannot be found or the Intent cannot be resolved to a component, NameNotFoundException is thrown.</p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Parameters</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>intent</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>Intent</code>: The intent for which you would like to retrieve a banner.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/graphics/drawable/Drawable.html">Drawable</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">Returns the image of the banner, or null if the activity has no banner specified.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Throws</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.NameNotFoundException.html">PackageManager.NameNotFoundException</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">Thrown if the resources for application matching the given intent could not be loaded.</td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <div> 
       <p><b>See also:</b></p> 
       <ul class="nolist">
        <li><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#getActivityBanner(android.content.ComponentName)">getActivityBanner(ComponentName)</a></code></li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <a name="getActivityBanner(android.content.ComponentName)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-20"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">getActivityBanner</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 20</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">

     <a name="getActivityIcon(android.content.Intent)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-1"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">getActivityIcon</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 1</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/graphics/drawable/Drawable.html">Drawable</a> getActivityIcon (<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/Intent.html">Intent</a> intent)</pre> 
      <p>Retrieve the icon associated with an Intent. If intent.getClassName() is set, this simply returns the result of getActivityIcon(intent.getClassName()). Otherwise it resolves the intent's component and returns the icon associated with the resolved component. If intent.getClassName() cannot be found or the Intent cannot be resolved to a component, NameNotFoundException is thrown.</p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Parameters</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>intent</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>Intent</code>: The intent for which you would like to retrieve an icon.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/graphics/drawable/Drawable.html">Drawable</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">Returns the image of the icon, or the default activity icon if it could not be found. Does not return null.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Throws</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.NameNotFoundException.html">PackageManager.NameNotFoundException</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">Thrown if the resources for application matching the given intent could not be loaded.</td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <div> 
       <p><b>See also:</b></p>

<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/ActivityInfo.html">ActivityInfo</a> getActivityInfo (<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/ComponentName.html">ComponentName</a> component, 
                int flags)</pre>

      <p></p>

         <th colspan="2">Parameters</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>component</code></td>

        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>flags</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>int</code>: Additional option flags to modify the data returned.<p>Value is either <code>0</code> or combination of <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#GET_META_DATA">GET_META_DATA</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#GET_SHARED_LIBRARY_FILES">GET_SHARED_LIBRARY_FILES</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_ALL">MATCH_ALL</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DEFAULT_ONLY">MATCH_DEFAULT_ONLY</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DISABLED_COMPONENTS">MATCH_DISABLED_COMPONENTS</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DISABLED_UNTIL_USED_COMPONENTS">MATCH_DISABLED_UNTIL_USED_COMPONENTS</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DIRECT_BOOT_AWARE">MATCH_DIRECT_BOOT_AWARE</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DIRECT_BOOT_UNAWARE">MATCH_DIRECT_BOOT_UNAWARE</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_SYSTEM_ONLY">MATCH_SYSTEM_ONLY</a></code> or <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_UNINSTALLED_PACKAGES">MATCH_UNINSTALLED_PACKAGES</a></code>.</p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/ActivityInfo.html">ActivityInfo</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">An <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/ActivityInfo.html">ActivityInfo</a></code> containing information about the activity.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table>

        </tr>

     <a name="getApplicationEnabledSetting(java.lang.String)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-1"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">getApplicationEnabledSetting</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 1</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
int getApplicationEnabledSetting (<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> packageName)</pre> 
      <p>Return the enabled setting for an application. This returns the last value set by <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#setApplicationEnabledSetting(java.lang.String, int, int)">setApplicationEnabledSetting(String, int, int)</a></code>; in most cases this value will be <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#COMPONENT_ENABLED_STATE_DEFAULT">COMPONENT_ENABLED_STATE_DEFAULT</a></code> since the value originally specified in the manifest has not been modified.</p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Parameters</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>packageName</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>String</code>: The package name of the application to retrieve.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>int</code></td> 
         <td width="100%">Returns the current enabled state for the application.<p>Value is <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#COMPONENT_ENABLED_STATE_DEFAULT">COMPONENT_ENABLED_STATE_DEFAULT</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#COMPONENT_ENABLED_STATE_ENABLED">COMPONENT_ENABLED_STATE_ENABLED</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#COMPONENT_ENABLED_STATE_DISABLED">COMPONENT_ENABLED_STATE_DISABLED</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#COMPONENT_ENABLED_STATE_DISABLED_USER">COMPONENT_ENABLED_STATE_DISABLED_USER</a></code> or <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#COMPONENT_ENABLED_STATE_DISABLED_UNTIL_USED">COMPONENT_ENABLED_STATE_DISABLED_UNTIL_USED</a></code>.</p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Throws</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/IllegalArgumentException.html">IllegalArgumentException</a></code></td>

      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/ApplicationInfo.html">ApplicationInfo</a> getApplicationInfo (<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> packageName, 
                int flags)</pre> 
      <p>Retrieve all of the information we know about a particular package/application.</p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Parameters</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>packageName</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>String</code>: The full name (i.e. com.google.apps.contacts) of an application.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>flags</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>int</code>: Additional option flags to modify the data returned.<p>Value is either <code>0</code> or combination of <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#GET_META_DATA">GET_META_DATA</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#GET_SHARED_LIBRARY_FILES">GET_SHARED_LIBRARY_FILES</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_UNINSTALLED_PACKAGES">MATCH_UNINSTALLED_PACKAGES</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_SYSTEM_ONLY">MATCH_SYSTEM_ONLY</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DISABLED_COMPONENTS">MATCH_DISABLED_COMPONENTS</a></code> or <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DISABLED_UNTIL_USED_COMPONENTS">MATCH_DISABLED_UNTIL_USED_COMPONENTS</a></code>.</p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/ApplicationInfo.html">ApplicationInfo</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">An <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/ApplicationInfo.html">ApplicationInfo</a></code> containing information about the package. If flag <code>MATCH_UNINSTALLED_PACKAGES</code> is set and if the package is not found in the list of installed applications, the application information is retrieved from the list of uninstalled applications (which includes installed applications as well as applications with data directory i.e. applications which had been deleted with <code>DONT_DELETE_DATA</code> flag set).<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Throws</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.NameNotFoundException.html">PackageManager.NameNotFoundException</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">if a package with the given name cannot be found on the system. </td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table>

     <div class="api apilevel-1"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">getDrawable</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 1</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/graphics/drawable/Drawable.html">Drawable</a> getDrawable (<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> packageName, 
                int resid, 
                <a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/ApplicationInfo.html">ApplicationInfo</a> appInfo)</pre> 
      <p>Retrieve an image from a package. This is a low-level API used by the various package manager info structures (such as <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/ComponentInfo.html">ComponentInfo</a></code> to implement retrieval of their associated icon.</p>

        </tr>

         <td width="100%"> <code>int</code>: The resource identifier of the desired image. Cannot be 0.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>appInfo</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>ApplicationInfo</code>: Overall information about <var>packageName</var>. This may be null, in which case the application information will be retrieved for you if needed; if you already have this information around, it can be much more efficient to supply it here.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table>

       <tbody>
        <tr>

        </tr>

     <a name="getInstalledApplications(int)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-1"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">getInstalledApplications</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 1</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/util/List.html">List</a>&lt;<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/ApplicationInfo.html">ApplicationInfo</a>&gt; getInstalledApplications (int flags)</pre> 
      <p>Return a List of all application packages that are installed on the device. If flag GET_UNINSTALLED_PACKAGES has been set, a list of all applications including those deleted with <code>DONT_DELETE_DATA</code> (partially installed apps with data directory) will be returned.</p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Parameters</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>flags</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>int</code>: Additional option flags to modify the data returned.<p>Value is either <code>0</code> or combination of <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#GET_META_DATA">GET_META_DATA</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#GET_SHARED_LIBRARY_FILES">GET_SHARED_LIBRARY_FILES</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_UNINSTALLED_PACKAGES">MATCH_UNINSTALLED_PACKAGES</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_SYSTEM_ONLY">MATCH_SYSTEM_ONLY</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DISABLED_COMPONENTS">MATCH_DISABLED_COMPONENTS</a></code> or <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DISABLED_UNTIL_USED_COMPONENTS">MATCH_DISABLED_UNTIL_USED_COMPONENTS</a></code>.</p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/util/List.html">List</a>&lt;<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/ApplicationInfo.html">ApplicationInfo</a>&gt;</code></td> 
         <td width="100%">A List of ApplicationInfo objects, one for each installed application. In the unlikely case there are no installed packages, an empty list is returned. If flag <code>MATCH_UNINSTALLED_PACKAGES</code> is set, the application information is retrieved from the list of uninstalled applications (which includes installed applications as well as applications with data directory i.e. applications which had been deleted with <code>DONT_DELETE_DATA</code> flag set). <p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
     </div> 
     <a name="getInstalledPackages(int)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-1"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">getInstalledPackages</h3>

     <a name="getInstantAppCookie()"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-26"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">getInstantAppCookie</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 26</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
byte[] getInstantAppCookie ()</pre> 
      <p>Gets the instant application cookie for this app. Non instant apps and apps that were instant but were upgraded to normal apps can still access this API. For instant apps this cookie is cached for some time after uninstall while for normal apps the cookie is deleted after the app is uninstalled. The cookie is always present while the app is installed.</p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>byte[]</code></td> 
         <td width="100%">The cookie.<p>This value will never be <code>null</code>.</p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <div>

     <a name="getLaunchIntentForPackage(java.lang.String)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-3"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">getLaunchIntentForPackage</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 3</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/Intent.html">Intent</a> getLaunchIntentForPackage (<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> packageName)</pre> 
      <p>Returns a "good" intent to launch a front-door activity in a package. This is used, for example, to implement an "open" button when browsing through packages. The current implementation looks first for a main activity in the category <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/Intent.html#CATEGORY_INFO">CATEGORY_INFO</a></code>, and next for a main activity in the category <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/Intent.html#CATEGORY_LAUNCHER">CATEGORY_LAUNCHER</a></code>. Returns <code>null</code> if neither are found.</p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Parameters</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>packageName</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>String</code>: The name of the package to inspect.<p>This value must never be <code>null</code>.</p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/Intent.html">Intent</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">A fully-qualified <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/Intent.html">Intent</a></code> that can be used to launch the main activity in the package. Returns <code>null</code> if the package does not contain such an activity, or if <em>packageName</em> is not recognized. <p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
     </div>

<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> getNameForUid (int uid)</pre> 
      <p>Retrieve the official name associated with a uid. This name is guaranteed to never change, though it is possible for the underlying uid to be changed.      <a name="getPackageGids(java.lang.String)"></a>

      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">

      <p>Return an array of all of the POSIX secondary group IDs that have been assigned to the given package. </p>
      <p> Note that the same package may have different GIDs under different <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/os/UserHandle.html">UserHandle</a></code> on the same device.</p>

        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>int[]</code></td> 
         <td width="100%">Returns an int array of the assigned GIDs, or null if there are none.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table>

       <tbody>

         <td width="100%">if a package with the given name cannot be found on the system. </td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>

     <a name="getPackageGids(java.lang.String, int)"></a>

      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">

                int flags)</pre> 
      <p>Return an array of all of the POSIX secondary group IDs that have been assigned to the given package. </p>
      <p> Note that the same package may have different GIDs under different <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/os/UserHandle.html">UserHandle</a></code> on the same device.</p>
      <p></p>

        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>flags</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>int</code> 
          <!-- no parameter comment --><p>Value is either <code>0</code> or combination of <code><a      <a name="getPackageInfo(android.content.pm.VersionedPackage, int)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-26"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">getPackageInfo</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 26</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageInfo.html">PackageInfo</a> getPackageInfo (<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/VersionedPackage.html">VersionedPackage</a> versionedPackage, 
                int flags)</pre> 
      <p>Retrieve overall information about an application package that is installed on the system. This method can be used for retrieving information about packages for which multiple versions can be installed at the time. Currently only packages hosting static shared libraries can have multiple installed versions. The method can also be used to get info for a package that has a single version installed by passing <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#VERSION_CODE_HIGHEST">VERSION_CODE_HIGHEST</a></code> in the <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/VersionedPackage.html">VersionedPackage</a></code> constructor.</p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Parameters</th>
        </tr>

         <td><code>versionedPackage</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>VersionedPackage</code>: The versioned package for which to query.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>flags</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>int</code>: Additional option flags to modify the data returned.<p>Value is either <code>0</code> or combination of <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#GET_ACTIVITIES">GET_ACTIVITIES</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#GET_CONFIGURATIONS">GET_CONFIGURATIONS</a></code>, <code><a      <a name="getPackagesForUid(int)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-1"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">getPackagesForUid</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 1</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String[]</a> getPackagesForUid (int uid)</pre> 
      <p>Retrieve the names of all packages that are associated with a particular user id. In most cases, this will be a single package name, the package that has been assigned that user id. Where there are multiple packages sharing the same user id through the "sharedUserId" mechanism, all packages with that id will be returned.</p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Parameters</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>uid</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>int</code>: The user id for which you would like to retrieve the associated packages.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String[]</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">Returns an array of one or more packages assigned to the user id, or null if there are no known packages with the given id. <p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
     </div>

href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#GET_SHARED_LIBRARY_FILES">GET_SHARED_LIBRARY_FILES</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#GET_SIGNATURES">GET_SIGNATURES</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#GET_URI_PERMISSION_PATTERNS">GET_URI_PERMISSION_PATTERNS</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_UNINSTALLED_PACKAGES">MATCH_UNINSTALLED_PACKAGES</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DISABLED_COMPONENTS">MATCH_DISABLED_COMPONENTS</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DISABLED_UNTIL_USED_COMPONENTS">MATCH_DISABLED_UNTIL_USED_COMPONENTS</a></code> or <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_SYSTEM_ONLY">MATCH_SYSTEM_ONLY</a></code>.</p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/util/List.html">List</a>&lt;<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageInfo.html">PackageInfo</a>&gt;</code></td> 
         <td width="100%">A List of PackageInfo objects, one for each installed package that holds any of the permissions that were provided, containing information about the package. If no installed packages hold any of the permissions, an empty list is returned. If flag <code>MATCH_UNINSTALLED_PACKAGES</code> is set, the package information is retrieved from the list of uninstalled applications (which includes installed applications as well as applications with data directory i.e. applications which had been deleted with <code>DONT_DELETE_DATA</code> flag set). <p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
     </div>

         <td width="100%"> <code>String</code>: An optional package in which you would like to limit the list. If null, all activities will be returned; if non-null, only those activities in the given package are returned.<p></p></td>

        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table>

     <a name="getResourcesForActivity(android.content.ComponentName)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-1"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">getResourcesForActivity</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 1</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/res/Resources.html">Resources</a> getResourcesForActivity (<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/ComponentName.html">ComponentName</a> activityName)</pre> 
      <p>Retrieve the resources associated with an activity. Given the full name of an activity, retrieves the information about it and calls getResources() to return its application's resources. If the activity cannot be found, NameNotFoundException is thrown.</p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Parameters</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr>

        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/res/Resources.html">Resources</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">Returns the application's Resources.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Throws</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.NameNotFoundException.html">PackageManager.NameNotFoundException</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">Thrown if the resources for the given application could not be loaded.</td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <div>

     <a name="getResourcesForApplication(java.lang.String)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-1"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">getResourcesForApplication</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 1</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/res/Resources.html">Resources</a> getResourcesForApplication (<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> appPackageName)</pre> 
      <p>Retrieve the resources associated with an application. Given the full package name of an application, retrieves the information about it and calls getResources() to return its application's resources. If the appPackageName cannot be found, NameNotFoundException is thrown.</p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Parameters</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>appPackageName</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>String</code>: Package name of the application whose resources are to be retrieved.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/res/Resources.html">Resources</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">Returns the application's Resources.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Throws</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.NameNotFoundException.html">PackageManager.NameNotFoundException</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">Thrown if the resources for the given application could not be loaded.</td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <div> 
       <p><b>See also:</b></p> 
       <ul class="nolist">
        <li><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#getResourcesForApplication(android.content.pm.ApplicationInfo)">getResourcesForApplication(ApplicationInfo)</a></code></li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
     </div>

     <a name="getText(java.lang.String, int, android.content.pm.ApplicationInfo)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-1"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">getText</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 1</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/CharSequence.html">CharSequence</a> getText (<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> packageName, 
                int resid, 
                <a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/ApplicationInfo.html">ApplicationInfo</a> appInfo)</pre> 
      <p>Retrieve text from a package. This is a low-level API used by the various package manager info structures (such as <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/ComponentInfo.html">ComponentInfo</a></code> to implement retrieval of their associated labels and other text.</p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Parameters</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>packageName</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>String</code>: The name of the package that this text is coming from. Cannot be null.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>resid</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>int</code>: The resource identifier of the desired text. Cannot be 0.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>appInfo</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>ApplicationInfo</code>: Overall information about <var>packageName</var>. This may be null, in which case the application information will be retrieved for you if needed; if you already have this information around, it can be much more efficient to supply it here.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/CharSequence.html">CharSequence</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">Returns a CharSequence holding the requested text. Returns null if the text could not be found for any reason. <p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
     </div> 
     <a name="getUserBadgedDrawableForDensity(android.graphics.drawable.Drawable, android.os.UserHandle, android.graphics.Rect, int)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-21"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">getUserBadgedDrawableForDensity</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 21</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/graphics/drawable/Drawable.html">Drawable</a> getUserBadgedDrawableForDensity (<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/graphics/drawable/Drawable.html">Drawable</a> drawable, 
                <a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/os/UserHandle.html">UserHandle</a> user, 
                <a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/graphics/Rect.html">Rect</a> badgeLocation, 
                int badgeDensity)</pre> 
      <p>If the target user is a managed profile of the calling user or the caller is itself a managed profile, then this returns a badged copy of the given drawable allowing the user to distinguish it from the original drawable. The caller can specify the location in the bounds of the drawable to be badged where the badge should be applied as well as the density of the badge to be used. </p>
      <p> If the original drawable is a BitmapDrawable and the backing bitmap is mutable as per <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/graphics/Bitmap.html#isMutable()">isMutable()</a></code>, the badging is performed in place and the original drawable is returned. </p>
      <p></p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Parameters</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>drawable</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>Drawable</code>: The drawable to badge.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>user</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>UserHandle</code>: The target user.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>badgeLocation</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>Rect</code>: Where in the bounds of the badged drawable to place the badge. If it's <code>null</code>, the badge is applied on top of the entire drawable being badged.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>badgeDensity</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>int</code>: The optional desired density for the badge as per <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/util/DisplayMetrics.html#densityDpi">densityDpi</a></code>. If it's not positive, the density of the display is used.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/graphics/drawable/Drawable.html">Drawable</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">A drawable that combines the original drawable and a badge as determined by the system. <p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
     </div> 
     <a name="getUserBadgedIcon(android.graphics.drawable.Drawable, android.os.UserHandle)"></a>

For badging an arbitrary drawable use <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#getUserBadgedDrawableForDensity(android.graphics.drawable.Drawable, android.os.UserHandle, android.graphics.Rect, int)">getUserBadgedDrawableForDensity(android.graphics.drawable.Drawable, UserHandle, android.graphics.Rect, int)</a></code>. </p>
      <p> If the original drawable is a BitmapDrawable and the backing bitmap is mutable as per <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/graphics/Bitmap.html#isMutable()">isMutable()</a></code>, the badging is performed in place and the original drawable is returned. </p>
