     <a name="hasSystemFeature(java.lang.String)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-5"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">hasSystemFeature</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 5</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
boolean hasSystemFeature (<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> name)</pre> 
      <p>Check whether the given feature name is one of the available features as returned by <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#getSystemAvailableFeatures()">getSystemAvailableFeatures()</a></code>. This tests for the presence of <em>any</em> version of the given feature name; use <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#hasSystemFeature(java.lang.String, int)">hasSystemFeature(String, int)</a></code> to check for a minimum version.</p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Parameters</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>name</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>String</code> 
          <!-- no parameter comment --><p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>boolean</code></td> 
         <td width="100%">Returns true if the devices supports the feature, else false. <p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
     </div> 
     <a name="hasSystemFeature(java.lang.String, int)"></a>

      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in

       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
boolean hasSystemFeature (<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> name, 
                int version)</pre> 
      <p>Check whether the given feature name and version is one of the available features as returned by <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#getSystemAvailableFeatures()">getSystemAvailableFeatures()</a></code>. Since features are defined to always be backwards compatible, this returns true if the available feature version is greater than or equal to the requested version.</p>
      <p></p>

     <a name="isPermissionRevokedByPolicy(java.lang.String, java.lang.String)"></a>

      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>

      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
boolean isPermissionRevokedByPolicy (<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> permName, 
                <a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> pkgName)</pre> 
      <p>Checks whether a particular permissions has been revoked for a package by policy. Typically the device owner or the profile owner may apply such a policy. The user cannot grant policy revoked permissions, hence the only way for an app to get such a permission is by a policy change.</p>
      <p></p>

        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>pkgName</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>String</code>: The name of the package you are checking against.<p>This value must never be <code>null</code>.</p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr>

        </tr>

        </tr>

       <tbody>

        </tr>

         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/util/List.html">List</a>&lt;<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/ResolveInfo.html">ResolveInfo</a>&gt;</code></td> 
         <td width="100%">Returns a List of ResolveInfo objects containing one entry for each matching receiver, ordered from best to worst. If there are no matching receivers, an empty list or null is returned. <p></p></td>

     <a name="queryIntentActivities(android.content.Intent, int)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-1"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">queryIntentActivities</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 1</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/util/List.html">List</a>&lt;<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/ResolveInfo.html">ResolveInfo</a>&gt; queryIntentActivities (<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/Intent.html">Intent</a> intent, 
                int flags)</pre> 
      <p>Retrieve all activities that can be performed for the given intent.</p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Parameters</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>intent</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>Intent</code>: The desired intent as per resolveActivity().<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>flags</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>int</code>: Additional option flags to modify the data returned. The most important is <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DEFAULT_ONLY">MATCH_DEFAULT_ONLY</a></code>, to limit the resolution to only those activities that support the <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/Intent.html#CATEGORY_DEFAULT">CATEGORY_DEFAULT</a></code>. Or, set <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_ALL">MATCH_ALL</a></code> to prevent any filtering of the results.<p>Value is either <code>0</code> or combination of <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#GET_META_DATA">GET_META_DATA</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#GET_SIGNATURES">GET_SIGNATURES</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#GET_SHARED_LIBRARY_FILES">GET_SHARED_LIBRARY_FILES</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_ALL">MATCH_ALL</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DISABLED_COMPONENTS">MATCH_DISABLED_COMPONENTS</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DISABLED_UNTIL_USED_COMPONENTS">MATCH_DISABLED_UNTIL_USED_COMPONENTS</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DEFAULT_ONLY">MATCH_DEFAULT_ONLY</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DIRECT_BOOT_AWARE">MATCH_DIRECT_BOOT_AWARE</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DIRECT_BOOT_UNAWARE">MATCH_DIRECT_BOOT_UNAWARE</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_SYSTEM_ONLY">MATCH_SYSTEM_ONLY</a></code> or <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_UNINSTALLED_PACKAGES">MATCH_UNINSTALLED_PACKAGES</a></code>.</p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/util/List.html">List</a>&lt;<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/ResolveInfo.html">ResolveInfo</a>&gt;</code></td> 
         <td width="100%">Returns a List of ResolveInfo objects containing one entry for each matching activity, ordered from best to worst. In other words, the first item is what would be returned by <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#resolveActivity(android.content.Intent, int)">resolveActivity(Intent, int)</a></code>. If there are no matching activities, an empty list is returned. <p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
     </div> 
     <a name="queryIntentActivityOptions(android.content.ComponentName, android.content.Intent[], android.content.Intent, int)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-1"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">queryIntentActivityOptions</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 1</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/util/List.html">List</a>&lt;<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/ResolveInfo.html">ResolveInfo</a>&gt; queryIntentActivityOptions (<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/ComponentName.html">ComponentName</a> caller, 
                <a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/Intent.html">Intent[]</a> specifics, 
                <a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/Intent.html">Intent</a> intent, 
                int flags)</pre> 
      <p>Retrieve a set of activities that should be presented to the user as similar options. This is like <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#queryIntentActivities(android.content.Intent, int)">queryIntentActivities(Intent, int)</a></code>, except it also allows you to supply a list of more explicit Intents that you would like to resolve to particular options, and takes care of returning the final ResolveInfo list in a reasonable order, with no duplicates, based on those inputs.</p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Parameters</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>caller</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>ComponentName</code>: The class name of the activity that is making the request. This activity will never appear in the output list. Can be null.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>specifics</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>Intent</code>: An array of Intents that should be resolved to the first specific results. Can be null.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>intent</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>Intent</code>: The desired intent as per resolveActivity().<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>flags</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>int</code>: Additional option flags to modify the data returned. The most important is <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DEFAULT_ONLY">MATCH_DEFAULT_ONLY</a></code>, to limit the resolution to only those activities that support the <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/Intent.html#CATEGORY_DEFAULT">CATEGORY_DEFAULT</a></code>.<p>Value is either <code>0</code> or combination of <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#GET_META_DATA">GET_META_DATA</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#GET_SIGNATURES">GET_SIGNATURES</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#GET_SHARED_LIBRARY_FILES">GET_SHARED_LIBRARY_FILES</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_ALL">MATCH_ALL</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DISABLED_COMPONENTS">MATCH_DISABLED_COMPONENTS</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DISABLED_UNTIL_USED_COMPONENTS">MATCH_DISABLED_UNTIL_USED_COMPONENTS</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DEFAULT_ONLY">MATCH_DEFAULT_ONLY</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DIRECT_BOOT_AWARE">MATCH_DIRECT_BOOT_AWARE</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DIRECT_BOOT_UNAWARE">MATCH_DIRECT_BOOT_UNAWARE</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_SYSTEM_ONLY">MATCH_SYSTEM_ONLY</a></code> or <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_UNINSTALLED_PACKAGES">MATCH_UNINSTALLED_PACKAGES</a></code>.</p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/util/List.html">List</a>&lt;<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/ResolveInfo.html">ResolveInfo</a>&gt;</code></td> 
         <td width="100%">Returns a List of ResolveInfo objects containing one entry for each matching activity. The list is ordered first by all of the intents resolved in <var>specifics</var> and then any additional activities that can handle <var>intent</var> but did not get included by one of the <var>specifics</var> intents. If there are no matching activities, an empty list is returned. <p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
     </div>

     <a name="resolveActivity(android.content.Intent, int)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-1"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">resolveActivity</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 1</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/ResolveInfo.html">ResolveInfo</a> resolveActivity (<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/Intent.html">Intent</a> intent, 
                int flags)</pre> 
      <p>Determine the best action to perform for a given Intent. This is how <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/Intent.html#resolveActivity(android.content.pm.PackageManager)">resolveActivity(PackageManager)</a></code> finds an activity if a class has not been explicitly specified. </p>
      <p> <em>Note:</em> if using an implicit Intent (without an explicit ComponentName specified), be sure to consider whether to set the <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DEFAULT_ONLY">MATCH_DEFAULT_ONLY</a></code> only flag. You need to do so to resolve the activity in the same way that <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/Context.html#startActivity(android.content.Intent)">startActivity(Intent)</a></code> and <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/Intent.html#resolveActivity(android.content.pm.PackageManager)">Intent.resolveActivity(PackageManager)</a></code> do. </p>
      <p></p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Parameters</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>intent</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>Intent</code>: An intent containing all of the desired specification (action, data, type, category, and/or component).<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>flags</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>int</code>: Additional option flags to modify the data returned. The most important is <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DEFAULT_ONLY">MATCH_DEFAULT_ONLY</a></code>, to limit the resolution to only those activities that support the <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/Intent.html#CATEGORY_DEFAULT">CATEGORY_DEFAULT</a></code>.<p>Value is either <code>0</code> or combination of <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#GET_META_DATA">GET_META_DATA</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#GET_SIGNATURES">GET_SIGNATURES</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#GET_SHARED_LIBRARY_FILES">GET_SHARED_LIBRARY_FILES</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_ALL">MATCH_ALL</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DISABLED_COMPONENTS">MATCH_DISABLED_COMPONENTS</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DISABLED_UNTIL_USED_COMPONENTS">MATCH_DISABLED_UNTIL_USED_COMPONENTS</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DEFAULT_ONLY">MATCH_DEFAULT_ONLY</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DIRECT_BOOT_AWARE">MATCH_DIRECT_BOOT_AWARE</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DIRECT_BOOT_UNAWARE">MATCH_DIRECT_BOOT_UNAWARE</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_SYSTEM_ONLY">MATCH_SYSTEM_ONLY</a></code> or <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_UNINSTALLED_PACKAGES">MATCH_UNINSTALLED_PACKAGES</a></code>.</p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/ResolveInfo.html">ResolveInfo</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">Returns a ResolveInfo object containing the final activity intent that was determined to be the best action. Returns null if no matching activity was found. If multiple matching activities are found and there is no default set, returns a ResolveInfo object containing something else, such as the activity resolver. <p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
     </div> 
     <a name="resolveContentProvider(java.lang.String, int)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-1"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">resolveContentProvider</h3> 
      <div class="api-level">

         added in

      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/ProviderInfo.html">ProviderInfo</a> resolveContentProvider (<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> name, 
                int flags)</pre> 
      <p>Find a single content provider by its base path name.</p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>

         <td><code>flags</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>int</code>: Additional option flags to modify the data returned.<p>Value is either <code>0</code> or combination of <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#GET_META_DATA">GET_META_DATA</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#GET_SHARED_LIBRARY_FILES">GET_SHARED_LIBRARY_FILES</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_ALL">MATCH_ALL</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DEFAULT_ONLY">MATCH_DEFAULT_ONLY</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DISABLED_COMPONENTS">MATCH_DISABLED_COMPONENTS</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DISABLED_UNTIL_USED_COMPONENTS">MATCH_DISABLED_UNTIL_USED_COMPONENTS</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DIRECT_BOOT_AWARE">MATCH_DIRECT_BOOT_AWARE</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_DIRECT_BOOT_UNAWARE">MATCH_DIRECT_BOOT_UNAWARE</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_SYSTEM_ONLY">MATCH_SYSTEM_ONLY</a></code> or <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#MATCH_UNINSTALLED_PACKAGES">MATCH_UNINSTALLED_PACKAGES</a></code>.</p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Returns</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/ProviderInfo.html">ProviderInfo</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">A <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/ProviderInfo.html">ProviderInfo</a></code> object containing information about the provider. If a provider was not found, returns null. <p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table>

     <a name="setApplicationCategoryHint(java.lang.String, int)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-26"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">setApplicationCategoryHint</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>

      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
void setApplicationCategoryHint (<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> packageName, 
                int categoryHint)</pre> 
      <p>Provide a hint of what the <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/ApplicationInfo.html#category">category</a></code> value should be for the given package. </p>
      <p> This hint can only be set by the app which installed this package, as determined by <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#getInstallerPackageName(java.lang.String)">getInstallerPackageName(String)</a></code>.</p>
      <p></p>

        </tr>

        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>categoryHint</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>int</code>: the category hint to set. <p>Value is <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/ApplicationInfo.html#CATEGORY_UNDEFINED">CATEGORY_UNDEFINED</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/ApplicationInfo.html#CATEGORY_GAME">CATEGORY_GAME</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/ApplicationInfo.html#CATEGORY_AUDIO">CATEGORY_AUDIO</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/ApplicationInfo.html#CATEGORY_VIDEO">CATEGORY_VIDEO</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/ApplicationInfo.html#CATEGORY_IMAGE">CATEGORY_IMAGE</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/ApplicationInfo.html#CATEGORY_SOCIAL">CATEGORY_SOCIAL</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/ApplicationInfo.html#CATEGORY_NEWS">CATEGORY_NEWS</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/ApplicationInfo.html#CATEGORY_MAPS">CATEGORY_MAPS</a></code> or <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/ApplicationInfo.html#CATEGORY_PRODUCTIVITY">CATEGORY_PRODUCTIVITY</a></code>.</p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table>

     <a name="setApplicationEnabledSetting(java.lang.String, int, int)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-1"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">setApplicationEnabledSetting</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 1</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
void setApplicationEnabledSetting (<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> packageName, 
                int newState, 
                int flags)</pre> 
      <p>Set the enabled setting for an application This setting will override any enabled state which may have been set by the application in its manifest. It also overrides the enabled state set in the manifest for any of the application's components. It does not override any enabled state set by <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#setComponentEnabledSetting(android.content.ComponentName, int, int)">setComponentEnabledSetting(ComponentName, int, int)</a></code> for any of the application's components.</p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Parameters</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>packageName</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>String</code>: The package name of the application to enable<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>newState</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>int</code>: The new enabled state for the application.<p>Value is <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#COMPONENT_ENABLED_STATE_DEFAULT">COMPONENT_ENABLED_STATE_DEFAULT</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#COMPONENT_ENABLED_STATE_ENABLED">COMPONENT_ENABLED_STATE_ENABLED</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#COMPONENT_ENABLED_STATE_DISABLED">COMPONENT_ENABLED_STATE_DISABLED</a></code>, <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#COMPONENT_ENABLED_STATE_DISABLED_USER">COMPONENT_ENABLED_STATE_DISABLED_USER</a></code> or <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#COMPONENT_ENABLED_STATE_DISABLED_UNTIL_USED">COMPONENT_ENABLED_STATE_DISABLED_UNTIL_USED</a></code>.</p></td> 
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>flags</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>int</code>: Optional behavior flags. <p>Value is either <code>0</code> or <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#DONT_KILL_APP">DONT_KILL_APP</a></code>.</p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
     </div>

     <a name="setInstallerPackageName(java.lang.String, java.lang.String)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-11"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">setInstallerPackageName</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 11</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
void setInstallerPackageName (<a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> targetPackage, 
                <a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/String.html">String</a> installerPackageName)</pre> 
      <p>Change the installer associated with a given package. There are limitations on how the installer package can be changed; in particular: </p>
      <ul> 
       <li> A SecurityException will be thrown if <var>installerPackageName</var> is not signed with the same certificate as the calling application. </li>
       <li> A SecurityException will be thrown if <var>targetPackage</var> already has an installer package, and that installer package is not signed with the same certificate as the calling application. </li>
      </ul>
      <p></p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Parameters</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>targetPackage</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>String</code>: The installed package whose installer will be changed.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>installerPackageName</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>String</code>: The package name of the new installer. May be null to clear the association. <p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
     </div> 
     <a name="updateInstantAppCookie(byte[])"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-26"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">updateInstantAppCookie</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 26</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
void updateInstantAppCookie (byte[] cookie)</pre> 
      <p>Updates the instant application cookie for the calling app. Non instant apps and apps that were instant but were upgraded to normal apps can still access this API. For instant apps this cookie is cached for some time after uninstall while for normal apps the cookie is deleted after the app is uninstalled. The cookie is always present while the app is installed. The cookie size is limited by <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#getInstantAppCookieMaxBytes()">getInstantAppCookieMaxBytes()</a></code>. Passing <code>null</code> or an empty array clears the cookie. </p>
      <p></p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Parameters</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>cookie</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>byte</code>: The cookie data.<p>This value may be <code>null</code>.</p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Throws</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/IllegalArgumentException.html">IllegalArgumentException</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">if the array exceeds max cookie size. </td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <div> 
       <p><b>See also:</b></p> 
       <ul class="nolist">
        <li><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#isInstantApp()">isInstantApp()</a></code></li>
        <li><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#isInstantApp(java.lang.String)">isInstantApp(String)</a></code></li>
        <li><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#getInstantAppCookieMaxBytes()">getInstantAppCookieMaxBytes()</a></code></li>
        <li><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#getInstantAppCookie()">getInstantAppCookie()</a></code></li>
        <li><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#clearInstantAppCookie()">clearInstantAppCookie()</a></code></li> 
       </ul> 
      </div> 
     </div> 
     <a name="verifyPendingInstall(int, int)"></a> 
     <div class="api apilevel-14"> 
      <h3 class="api-name">verifyPendingInstall</h3> 
      <div class="api-level"> 
       <div>
         added in 
        <a href="https://developer.android.com/guide/topics/manifest/uses-sdk-element.html#ApiLevels">API level 14</a>
       </div> 
      </div> 
      <pre class="api-signature no-pretty-print">
void verifyPendingInstall (int id, 
                int verificationCode)</pre> 
      <p>Allows a package listening to the <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/Intent.html#ACTION_PACKAGE_NEEDS_VERIFICATION">package verification broadcast</a></code> to respond to the package manager. The response must include the <code>verificationCode</code> which is one of <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#VERIFICATION_ALLOW">VERIFICATION_ALLOW</a></code> or <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#VERIFICATION_REJECT">VERIFICATION_REJECT</a></code>.</p>
      <p></p> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Parameters</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>id</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>int</code>: pending package identifier as passed via the <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#EXTRA_VERIFICATION_ID">EXTRA_VERIFICATION_ID</a></code> Intent extra.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code>verificationCode</code></td> 
         <td width="100%"> <code>int</code>: either <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#VERIFICATION_ALLOW">VERIFICATION_ALLOW</a></code> or <code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageManager.html#VERIFICATION_REJECT">VERIFICATION_REJECT</a></code>.<p></p></td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
      <table class="responsive"> 
       <tbody>
        <tr>
         <th colspan="2">Throws</th>
        </tr> 
        <tr> 
         <td><code><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/java/lang/SecurityException.html">SecurityException</a></code></td> 
         <td width="100%">if the caller does not have the PACKAGE_VERIFICATION_AGENT permission. </td> 
        </tr> 
       </tbody>
      </table> 
     </div>

        <li class="api apilevel-1"><a href="https://developer.android.com/reference/android/content/pm/PackageStats.html">PackageStats</a></li>

       </ul> </li>

       <ul>
